[30/06/25, 8:00:26â€¯AM] Pooja-CREAI-Agent: Dear CREA(I) Members,

We are pleased to formally announce the CREA(I) Grievance Cell Procedures :-

The Grievance Cell is a key initiative by CREA (I) to uphold ethical, professional and fair business practices in the real estate industry. It offers a structured platform to address valid member concerns with transparency and impartiality.

 Grievance Committee

1. Mr. A.A. Sheriff â€“ Advisory Board Member
2. Mr. R.P. Agarwal â€“ Advisory Board Member
3. Ms. Sarla Menon â€“ Vice President

Types of Complaints Handled (Primary & Secondary Sales)

1ï¸âƒ£ Non-payment of commission by  Developers, Landlords, Tenants, Corporates, Individuals
across Residential, Commercial, Land (JV/Outright),Warehousing, Industrial & Agri segments

2ï¸âƒ£ Disputes between CREA (I) Members:
1. Property or client representation
â€ƒ2. Commission or service fee sharing

ğŸ“Œ Rules & Requirements
1. Only complaints supported by proper documentation (emails, agreements, etc.) will be considered
2. Sub judice/legal matters will not be entertained

 Grievance Resolution Fee Policy:
To maintain the integrity and efficiency of the grievance process:

Fee: â‚¹10,000/- (Rupees Ten Thousand Only) plus applicable GST,
Payable To: CREA (I)
Mandatory: Fee must be paid before the grievance is taken up.

Applicable For:
1. Disputes with Developers, Landlords, Corporates, and Clients

2. Member-to-member grievances

Note: This fee is non-refundable, regardless of the outcome.

Standard Procedure (Primary Sales: Channel Partners & Developers)

1. All communication must be in writing (email/formal documentation)

2. CPs must have a signed agreement with the developer outlining business terms

3. Leads must be shared in writing with the Developer and site visits conducted only after their approval

4. Commission becomes payable upon clientâ€™s agreement payment (or as contractually agreed,
5. â Developer is supposed to clear CP's payment within 30-45 days of agreement signing,

6. In case of delay, escalate via email to the Developer & CC the Grievance Cell

7. If unresolved, submit full documentation to the Grievance Committee for review

For Commercial Leasing, JV Land, Warehousing, Industrial, or Agri Land Deals:
âœ”ï¸ Ensure a duly signed agreement with all parties
âœ”ï¸ For corporates, obtain company seal on documents wherever possible


We welcome constructive feedback to improve our systems.

Letâ€™s work together to ensure ethical, respectful, and professional real estate practices under the CREA(I) banner. ğŸ¤

Please share your concern with complete supporting documents at the official email ID below:
grievance@creaindia.in

Regards 
CREA (I) Committee

[30/06/25, 10:36:33â€¯AM] AA Sherrif --V-Chairman CREAI: Dear CREA(I) Members,

Thank you Ms Sarla Menon for formalizing the **CREA(I) Grievance Cell Procedures**, 
 As an Advisory Board Member, we wholeheartedly endorse this structured initiative to uphold ethics, transparency, and professionalism in our industry. This framework is a critical step toward resolving disputes fairly and preserving the integrity of CREA(I)â€™s mission.  


1. **Scope & Clarity**:  
   - Comprehensive coverage of grievances (non-payment, member disputes, cross-segment issues) ensures no valid concern falls through the cracks.  
   - Explicit documentation requirements will streamline resolutions and deter frivolous claims.  

2. **Fee Policy Rationale**:  
   - The â‚¹10,000 + GST fee underscores the seriousness of submissions while ensuring efficient resource allocation. I urge members to view this as an investment in credible dispute resolution.  

3. **Standardized Procedures**:  
   - Mandating written agreements , lead approvals, and payment timelines sets clear accountability benchmarks.  
   - Escalation protocols provide a pragmatic path for unresolved issues.  
 Member Advisory:  
- **Documentation is Non-Negotiable**: Secure signed agreements/client communications *proactively*. Delays often stem from poor record-keeping.  
- **Leverage the Cell Early**: Escalate *only after* exhausting direct resolution . 
This preserves relationships and Cell efficiency.  
- **Fee Transparency**: Members must budget for grievance costs. Consider this a safeguard against prolonged disputes.  

A Unified Call:  
Letâ€™s champion this Cell as a testament to CREA(I)â€™s commitment to fairness. I encourage every member to:  
- **Study Procedures**: Align operations with CREA(I)â€™s standards (e.g., written lead approvals).  
- **Share Feedback**: Collaborate to refine the framework as real-world cases emerge.  
- **Uphold Ethics**: Report grievances responsibly via **grievance@creaindia.in** *with complete evidence*.  

Together, we can transform industry practices. Well done to the Committee and Grievance Cell members especially Ms Sarla Menon , Chairman Emeritus Pradeep Joe, President Samir Arora for leading this vital effort.  

Regards,  
A A Sheriff.
Advisory Board Member, CREA(I) â€<This message was edited>
